199→\t\tt, err = sigv4.NewSigV4RoundTripper(conf.SigV4Config, t)\n   200→\t\tif err != nil {\n   201→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   202→\t\t}\n   203→\t}\n   204→\n   205→\tif conf.AzureADConfig != nil {\n   206→\t\tt, err = azuread.NewAzureADRoundTripper(conf.AzureADConfig, t)\n   207→\t\tif err != nil {\n   208→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   209→\t\t}\n   210→\t}\n   211→\n   212→\tif conf.GoogleIAMConfig != nil {\n   213→\t\tt, err = googleiam.NewRoundTripper(conf.GoogleIAMConfig, t)\n   214→\t\tif err != nil {\n   215→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   216→\t\t}\n   217→\t}\n   218→\n   219→\twriteProtoMsg := remoteapi.WriteV1MessageType\n   220→\tif conf.WriteProtoMsg != \"\" {\n   221→\t\twriteProtoMsg = conf.WriteProtoMsg\n   222→\t}\n   223→\thttpClient.Transport = otelhttp.NewTransport(\n   224→\t\tt,\n   225→\t\totelhttp.WithClientTrace(func(ctx context.Context) *httptrace.ClientTrace {\n   226→\t\t\treturn otelhttptrace.NewClientTrace(ctx, otelhttptrace.WithoutSubSpans())\n   227→\t\t}))\n   228→\n   229→\treturn &Client{\n   230→\t\tremoteName:       name,\n   231→\t\turlString:        conf.URL.String(),\n   232→\t\tClient:           httpClient,\n   233→\t\tretryOnRateLimit: conf.RetryOnRateLimit,\n   234→\t\ttimeout:          time.Duration(conf.Timeout),\n   235→\t\twriteProtoMsg:    writeProtoMsg,\n   236→\t\twriteCompression: remoteapi.SnappyBlockCompression,\n   237→\t}, nil\n   238→}\n   239→\n   240→func newInjectHeadersRoundTripper(h map[string]string, underlyingRT http.RoundTripper) *injectHeadersRoundTripper {\n   241→\treturn &injectHeadersRoundTripper{headers: h, RoundTripper: underlyingRT}\n   242→}\n   243→\n   244→type injectHeadersRoundTripper struct {\n   245→\theaders map[string]string\n   246→\thttp.RoundTripper\n   247→}\n   248→\n   249→func (t *injectHeadersRoundTripper) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {\n   250→\tfor key, value := range t.headers {\n   251→\t\treq.Header.Set(key, value)\n   252→\t}\n   253→\treturn t.RoundTripper.RoundTrip(req)\n   254→}\n   255→\n   256→const defaultBackoff = 0\n   257→\n   258→type RecoverableError struct {\n   259→\terror\n   260→\tretryAfter model.Duration\n   261→}\n   262→\n   263→// Store sends a batch of samples to the HTTP endpoint, the request is the proto marshalled\n   264→// and encoded bytes from codec.go.\n   265→func (c *Client) Store(ctx context.Context, req []byte, attempt int) (WriteResponseStats, error) {\n   266→\thttpReq, err := http.NewRequest(http.MethodPost, c.urlString, bytes.NewReader(req))\n   267→\tif err != nil {\n   268→\t\t// Errors from NewRequest are from unparsable URLs, so are not\n   269→\t\t// recoverable.\n   270→\t\treturn WriteResponseStats{}, err\n   271→\t}\n   272→\n   273→\thttpReq.Header.Add(\"Content-Encoding\", string(c.writeCompression))\n   274→\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"Content-Type\", remoteWriteContentTypeHeaders[c.writeProtoMsg])\n   275→\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"User-Agent\", UserAgent)\n   276→\tif c.writeProtoMsg == remoteapi.WriteV1MessageType {\n   277→\t\t// Compatibility mode for 1.0.\n   278→\t\thttpReq.Header.Set(RemoteWriteVersionHeader, RemoteWriteVersion1HeaderValue)\n   279→\t} else {\n   280→\t\thttpReq.Header.Set(RemoteWriteVersionHeader, RemoteWriteVersion20HeaderValue)\n   281→\t}\n   282→\n   283→\tif attempt > 0 {\n   284→\t\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"Retry-Attempt\", strconv.Itoa(attempt))\n   285→\t}\n   286→\n   287→\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, c.timeout)\n   288→\tdefer cancel()\n   289→\n   290→\tctx, span := otel.Tracer(\"\").Start(ctx, \"Remote Store\", trace.WithSpanKind(trace.SpanKindClient))\n   291→\tdefer span.End()\n   292→\n   293→\thttpResp, err := c.Client.Do(httpReq.WithContext(ctx))\n   294→\tif err != nil {\n   295→\t\t// Errors from Client.Do are from (for example) network errors, so are\n   296→\t\t// recoverable.\n   297→\t\treturn WriteResponseStats{}, RecoverableError{err, defaultBackoff}\n   298→\t}\n   299→\tdefer func() {\n   300→\t\t_, _ = io.Copy(io.Discard, httpResp.Body)\n   301→\t\t_ = httpResp.Body.Close()\n   302→\t}()\n   303→\n   304→\t// NOTE(bwplotka): Only PRW2 spec defines response HTTP headers. However, spec does not block\n   305→\t// PRW1 from sending them too for reliability. Support this case.\n   306→\t//\n   307→\t// TODO(bwplotka): Pass logger and emit debug on error?\n   308→\t// Parsing error means there were some response header values we can't parse,\n   309→\t// we can continue handling.\n   310→\trs, _ := ParseWriteResponseStats(httpResp)\n   311→\n   312→\tif httpResp.StatusCode/100 == 2 {\n   313→\t\treturn rs, nil\n   314→\t}\n   315→\n   316→\t// Handling errors e.g. read potential error in the body.\n   317→\t// TODO(bwplotka): Pass logger and emit debug on error?\n   318→\tbody, _ := io.ReadAll(io.LimitReader(httpResp.Body, maxErrMsgLen))\n   319→\terr = fmt.Errorf(\"server returned HTTP status %s: %s\", httpResp.Status, body)\n   320→\n   321→\tif httpResp.StatusCode/100 == 5 ||\n   322→\t\t(c.retryOnRateLimit && httpResp.StatusCode == http.StatusTooManyRequests) {\n   323→\t\treturn rs, RecoverableError{err, retryAfterDuration(httpResp.Header.Get(\"Retry-After\"))}\n   324→\t}\n   325→\treturn rs, err\n   326→}\n   327→\n   328→// retryAfterDuration returns the duration for the Retry-After header. In case of any errors, it\n   329→// returns the defaultBackoff as if the header was never supplied.\n   330→func retryAfterDuration(t string) model.Duration {\n   331→\tparsedDuration, err := time.Parse(http.TimeFormat, t)\n   332→\tif err == nil {\n   333→\t\ts := time.Until(parsedDuration).Seconds()\n   334→\t\treturn model.Duration(s) * model.Duration(time.Second)\n   335→\t}\n   336→\t// The duration can be in seconds.\n   337→\td, err := strconv.Atoi(t)\n   338→\tif err != nil {\n   339→\t\treturn defaultBackoff\n   340→\t}\n   341→\treturn model.Duration(d) * model.Duration(time.Second)\n   342→}\n   343→\n   344→// Name uniquely identifies the client.\n   345→func (c *Client) Name() string {\n   346→\treturn c.remoteName\n   347→}\n   348→\n   349→// Endpoint is the remote read or write endpoint.\n   350→func (c *Client) Endpoint() string {\n   351→\treturn c.urlString\n   352→}\n   353→\n   354→// Read reads from a remote endpoint. The sortSeries parameter is only respected in the case of a samples response;\n   355→// chunked responses arrive already sorted by the server.\n   356→func (c *Client) Read(ctx context.Context, query *prompb.Query, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error) {\n   357→\treturn c.ReadMultiple(ctx, []*prompb.Query{query}, sortSeries)\n   358→}\n   359→\n   360→// ReadMultiple reads from a remote endpoint using multiple queries in a single request.\n   361→// The sortSeries parameter is only respected in the case of a samples response;\n   362→// chunked responses arrive already sorted by the server.\n   363→// Returns a single SeriesSet with interleaved series from all queries.\n   364→func (c *Client) ReadMultiple(ctx context.Context, queries []*prompb.Query, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error) {\n   365→\tc.readQueries.Inc()\n   366→\tdefer c.readQueries.Dec()\n   367→\n   368→\treq := &prompb.ReadRequest{\n   369→\t\tQueries:               queries,\n   370→\t\tAcceptedResponseTypes: c.acceptedResponseTypes,\n   371→\t}\n   372→\n   373→\thttpResp, cancel, start, err := c.executeReadRequest(ctx, req)\n   374→\tif err != nil {\n   375→\t\treturn nil, for reading data.\n   382→func (c *Client) executeReadRequest(ctx context.Context, req *prompb.ReadRequest) (*http.Response, context.CancelFunc, time.Time, error) {\n   383→\tdata, err := proto.Marshal(req)\n   384→\tif err != nil {\n   385→\t\treturn nil, nil, time.Time{}, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to marshal read request: %w\", err)\n   386→\t}\n   387→\n   388→\tcompressed := 395→\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/x-protobuf\")\n   396→\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"User-Agent\", UserAgent)\n   397→\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"X-Prometheus-Remote-Read-Version\", \"0.1.0\")\n   398→\n   399→\terrTimeout := fmt.Errorf(\"%w: request timed out after %s\", context.DeadlineExceeded, c.timeout)\n   400→\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeoutCause(ctx, c.timeout, handleReadResponse(httpResp *http.Response, req *prompb.ReadRequest, queries []*prompb.Query, sortSeries bool, start time.Time, cancel context.CancelFunc) (storage.SeriesSet, error) {\n   417→\tif httpResp.StatusCode/100 != 2 {\n   418→\t\t// Make an attempt at getting an error message.\n   419→\t\tbody, _ := io.ReadAll(httpResp.Body)\n   420→\t\t_ = httpResp.Body.Close()\n   421→\n   422→\t\tcancel()\n   423→\t\terrStr := strings.Trim(string(body), \"\\n\")\n   424→\t\terr := errors.New(errStr)\n   425→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"remote server %s returned http status %s: %w\", c.urlString, httpResp.Status, err)\n   426→\t}\n   427→\n   428→\tcontentType := httpResp.Header.Get(\"Content-Type\")\n   429→\n   430→\tswitch {\n   431→\tcase strings.HasPrefix(contentType, \"application/x-protobuf\"):\n   432→\t\tc.readQueriesDuration.WithLabelValues(\"sampled\").Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds())\n   433→\t\tc.readQueriesTotal.WithLabelValues(\"sampled\", strconv.Itoa(httpResp.StatusCode)).Inc()\n   434→\t\tss, err := c.handleSampledResponse(req, httpResp, sortSeries)\n   435→\t\tcancel()\n   436→\t\treturn ss, err\n   437→\tcase strings.HasPrefix(contentType, \"application/x-streamed-protobuf; proto=prometheus.ChunkedReadResponse\"):\n   438→\t\tc.readQueriesDuration.WithLabelValues(\"chunked\").Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds())\n   439→\n   440→\t\ts := NewChunkedReader(httpResp.Body, c.chunkedReadLimit, nil)\n   441→\t\treturn \"aborted_stream\"\n   445→\t\t\t}\n   446→\t\t\tc.readQueriesTotal.WithLabelValues(\"chunked\", code).Inc()\n   447→\t\t\tcancel()\n   448→\t\t}), nil\n   449→\tdefault:\n   450→\t\tc.readQueriesDuration.WithLabelValues(\"unsupported\").Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds())\n   451→\t\tc.readQueriesTotal.WithLabelValues(\"unsupported\", strconv.Itoa(httpResp.StatusCode)).Inc()\n   452→\t\tcancel()\n   453→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unsupported content type: %s\", contentType)\n   454→\t}\n   455→}\n   456→\n   457→func (*Client) handleSampledResponse(req *prompb.ReadRequest, httpResp *http.Response, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error) {\n   458→\tcompressed, err := io.ReadAll(httpResp.Body)\n   459→\tif err != nil {\n   460→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error reading response. HTTP status code: %s: %w\", httpResp.Status, err)\n   461→\t}\n   462→\tdefer func() {\n   463→\t\t_, _ = io.Copy(io.Discard, httpResp.Body)\n   464→\t\t_ = httpResp.Body.Close()\n   465→\t}()\n   466→\n   467→\tuncompressed, err := snappy.Decode(nil, compressed)\n   468→\tif err != nil {\n   469→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error reading response: %w\", err)\n   470→\t}\n   471→\n   472→\tvar resp prompb.ReadResponse\n   473→\terr = proto.Unmarshal(uncompressed, &resp)\n   474→\tif err != nil {\n   475→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to unmarshal response body: %w\", err)\n   476→\t}\n   477→\n   478→\tif len(resp.Results) != len(req.Queries) {\n   479→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"responses: want %d, got %d\", len(req.Queries), len(resp.Results))\n   480→\t}\n   481→\n   482→\treturn combineQueryResults(resp.Results, sortSeries)\n   483→}\n   484→\n   485→// combineQueryResults combines multiple query results into a single SeriesSet,\n   486→// handling both sorted and unsorted cases appropriately.\n   487→func combineQueryResults(results []*prompb.QueryResult, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error) {\n   488→\tif len(results) == 0 {\n   489→\t\treturn &concreteSeriesSet{series: nil, cur: 0}, nil\n   490→\t}\n   491→\n   492→\tif len(results) == 1 {\n   493→\t\treturn FromQueryResult(sortSeries, results[0]), nil\n   494→\t}\n   495→\n   496→\t// Multiple queries case - combine all results\n   497→\tif sortSeries {\n   498→\t\t// When sorting is requested, use MergeSeriesSet which can efficiently merge sorted inputs\n   499→\t\tvar allSeriesSets []storage.SeriesSet\n   500→\t\tfor _, result := range results {\n   501→\t\t\tseriesSet := FromQueryResult(sortSeries, result)\n   502→\t\t\tif err := seriesSet.Err(); err != nil {\n   503→\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error reading series from query result: %w\", err)\n   504→\t\t\t}\n   505→\t\t\tallSeriesSets = append(allSeriesSets, seriesSet)\n   506→\t\t}\n   507→\t\treturn storage.NewMergeSeriesSet(allSeriesSets, 0, storage.ChainedSeriesMerge), nil\n   508→\t}\n   509→\n   510→\t// When sorting is not requested, just concatenate all series without using MergeSeriesSet\n   511→\t// since MergeSeriesSet requires sorted inputs\n   512→\tvar allSeries []storage.Series\n   513→\tfor _, result := range results {\n   514→\t\tseriesSet := FromQueryResult(sortSeries, result)\n   515→\t\tfor seriesSet.Next() {\n   516→\t\t\tallSeries = append(allSeries, seriesSet.At())\n   517→\t\t}\n   518→\t\tif err := seriesSet.Err(); err != nil {\n   519→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error reading series from query result: %w\", err)\n   520→\t\t}\n   521→\t}\n   522→\n   523→\treturn &concreteSeriesSet{series: allSeries, cur: 0}, nil\n   524→}\n   525→\n   526→// handleChunkedResponseImpl handles chunked responses for both single and multiple queries.\n   527→func (*Client) handleChunkedResponseImpl(s *ChunkedReader, httpResp *http.Response, queries []*prompb.Query, onClose func(error)) storage.SeriesSet {\n   528→\t// For multiple queries in chunked response, we'll still use the existing infrastructure\n   529→\t// but we need to provide the timestamp range that covers all queries\n   530→\tvar minStartTs, maxEndTs int64 = math.MaxInt64, math.MinInt64\n   531→\n   532→\tfor _, query := range queries {\n   533→\t\tminStartTs = min(minStartTs, query.StartTimestampMs)\n   534→\t\tmaxEndTs = max(maxEndTs, query.EndTimestampMs)\n   535→\t}\n   536→\n   537→\treturn NewChunkedSeriesSet(s, httpResp.Body, minStartTs, maxEndTs, onClose)\n   538→}\n   539→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. (ReadClient, error) {\n\thttpClient, err := config_util.NewClientFromConfig(conf.HTTPClientConfig, \"remote_storage_read_client\", optFuncs...)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tt :=
